# This file contains UnTranslated regions (UTR) of Transcription Units (TU) :
#    5' UTR : From transcription start site to one nucleotide before start codon of the first gene of TU
#    3' UTR : From one nucleotide after stop codon of the last gene of TU to last nucleotide of the terminator
#
# Columns:
# (1) Operon Name
# (2) Transcription Unit Name (TU)
# (3) Promoter Name
# (4) Transcription start site (+1)
# (5) DNA strand  of TU
# (6) First Gene Name of TU [Gene Position left, Gene Position right]
# (7) Last Gene Name of TU [Gene Position left, Gene Position right]
# (8) Terminator Type [Terminator Position left, Terminator Position right]
# (9) Coordinates of UTR [+1 OR Start of the first gene] to [End of the terminator OR End of the last gene]*
# (10) Coordinates 5' UTR
# (11) 5' UTR Sequence	
# (12) Coordinates 3' UTR
# (13) 3' UTR Sequence
#
# * When the first one is NULL the other field is used
#
